<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gryzti</i>. Non-Slavic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">ีฏึีฎีฅีด</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krcem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">๐บ๐๐น๐ฟ๐๐๐ฐ๐ฝ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kriustan</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">grate, grind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะณััะทัั.html>ะณััะทัั</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gryztสน</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ะฟัะพะณััฬะทัั</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ะฟะพะณััฬะทัั</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ัะณััะทัั</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gnaw</li>
<li>to nibble</li>
<li>to crack <i>(nuts)</i></li>
<li>to bite <i>(fingernails)</i></li>
<li>to nag at</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
